<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шалый.html>ша́лый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šályj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crazy, mad</li>
<li>stray <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bullet, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***шампунь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шампунь.html>шампу́нь</a> (18377)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shampooing</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">चाँपो</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cā̃po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шампунь.html>шампу́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šampúnʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шампунь.html>шампу́ня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шампунь.html>шампу́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шампунь.html>шампу́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shampoo</li></ol>

***шантрапа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шантрапа.html>шантрапа́</a> (32410)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The origin is uncertain. Originally a dialectal word.
</p><p>Perhaps connected with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/History_of_the_Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:History of the Czech language">Old Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-ocs">šantrok</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">šаntrосha</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheater</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">santrocke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fraud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p><p>Alternatively, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">chantera pas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">will not sing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, said about serfs' children which were not chosen for the landowner's choir.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шантрапа.html>шантрапа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šantrapá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шантрапа.html>шантрапы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шантрапа.html>шантрапы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шантрапа.html>шантра́п</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>worthless person</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шапка.html>ша́пка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šápka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шапочка.html>ша́почка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šápočka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шапочка.html>ша́почки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шапочка.html>ша́почки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шапочка.html>ша́почек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шапка.html>ша́пка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šápka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (small) hat</li></ol>

***шар.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шар</a> (2244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear. Perhaps related (although <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Max_Vasmer" class="extiw" title="w:Max Vasmer">Vasmer</a> found it unconvincing) to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">шаръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šarŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">color, paint</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">шарити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šariti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to paint</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">шаръчи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šarŭči</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">painter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which probably derive from an early <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing into Slavic; cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Turkic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Turkic language">Proto-Turkic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="trk-pro">*siarïg</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">yellow, white</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. In that case, the sense development might have been “color, paint” → “spot” → “round object”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шар</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šar</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>ша́ра</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шара́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шары́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шаро́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* After the numbers 2, 3 and 4, the stress in the genitive singular falls on the <b>final syllable</b>: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шара́</a></span>.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>ball, solid sphere</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ball <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the set of points lying within a given distance from a given point</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>balloon</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ша.html>ша</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хать<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:шарахнуться.html>шара́хнуться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-шарах-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарахнуть.html>шара́хнуть</a> (16943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">шара́хать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šaráxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарахнуть.html>шара́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šaráxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шара́хать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hit, to strike, to land a blow <i>(on)</i>, to sock, to paste one</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to boom, to shoot with a boom</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drink, to gulp down</li></ol>

***шарик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рик</a> (4686)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шар</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šárik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́риков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шар</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: small ball, bead
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рик</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подшипник.html>подши́пников</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šárik</b> dlja podšípnikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ball for bearings</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">нафтали́новый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рик</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naftalínovyj <b>šárik</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mothball</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рик</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мороженый.html>моро́женого</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šárik</b> moróženovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scoop of ice cream</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>corpuscle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of blood</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровяной.html>кровяны́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рики</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krásnyje krovjanýje <b>šáriki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">red blood corpuscles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> brains, mental ability
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рики</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ролик.html>ро́лики</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заехать.html>зае́хали</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>šáriki</b> za róliki zajéxali</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is off his rocker; he went a little zonkers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́риков</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>šárikov</b> ne xvatájet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has a few loose screws</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">he doesn't have enough ‘balls’/brains</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рик</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šárik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шариковый.html>ша́риковый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šárikovyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> small ball, bead
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шариковый.html>ша́риковая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ручка.html>ру́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šárikovaja</b> rúčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ballpoint pen</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шариковый.html>ша́риковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подшипник.html>подши́пник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šárikovyj</b> podšípnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ball bearing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарить.html>ша́рить</a> (5697)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарить.html>ша́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šáritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пошарить.html>поша́рить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fumble, to rummage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to understand, to have knowledge of, to know something well (<i>about activities</i>)</li>

***шарманка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарманка.html>шарма́нка</a> (25129)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the name of the first songs played by barrel organ - Charmante Catherine (<i>Charming Catherine</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарманка.html>шарма́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šarmánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарманка.html>шарма́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарманка.html>шарма́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шарманка.html>шарма́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>barrel organ</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> repetitious talk</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаровой.html>шарово́й</a> (24889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шар</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаровой.html>шарово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šarovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ball, globe; globular, spherical
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шаровой.html>шарова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молния.html>мо́лния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šarovája</b> mólnija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>ball</b> lightning</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шаровой.html>шарово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегмент.html>сегме́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šarovój</b> segmént</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>spherical</b> segment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шаровой.html>шарово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клапан.html>кла́пан</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šarovój</b> klápan</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>ball</b> valve</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шаровой.html>шарово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарнир.html>шарни́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šarovój</b> šarnír</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ball and socket joint</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>ball</b> joint</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шаровой.html>шарово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:манипулятор.html>манипуля́тор</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šarovój</b> manipuljátor</i> ― <span class="e-translation">trackball</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>ball</b> manipulator</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
